 chashmadid gagan se bhi nakaabposhon ke bare main jaankaree jutai ja rahi he
 Arun is also being called from Delhi
 purv bhartiya captain or purv mukhya chayankarta dilip vengsarakar kaa maananaa he ki haal main achche pradarshan ke baad bhartiya cricketer atmamugdhata kaa shikaar ho gaye or england ke khilaaf maujuuda test shrinkhalaa main yahi team ke kharaab pradarshan kaa ahm kaaran he
 Vengsarkar also believes that the team got very little time to prepare against the strong England team
 shrinkhalaa ke pehle do test dekhne england gaye vengsarakar ke saakshatkar ke ahm ansh
 Question: Did you expect the Indian team to perform so poorly
 team ke kharaab pradarshan kaa kya kaaran he jisane sirf chaar maheene pehle vishwa cap khitaab jeeta tha
 Vengsarkar: To be honest, i knew that it was going to be a difficult series for India because they had to face a strong team which is in rhythm and has been consistently doing well in recent times
 iske alaava unka gendbaaji akraman behatar tha or ek team ke rup main unhen shrinkhalaa kii taiyaari kaa kaaphi samay mila
 India, on the other hand, arrived after playing a busy series in the West Indies and got very little time to prepare and get in tune with England's conditions
 mujhe lagata he ki bharat pichley kuch satr main achche pradarshan ke baad atmamugdhata kaa shikaar ho gaya
 Q: Do you think that a bowler over-reliance on Zaheer Khan is not good for the team
 uttar: kya or koi vikalp maujuud he? hamen sweekaar karnaa hoga ki hamaare paas ballebaaji yaa gendbaaji main adhik vikalp nahin hai visheshkar jab ham majboot virdohi kaa saamana karte hai
 We are dependent on tested players even if they are coming back after injury and they don't have much match practice
 aap is tarah pratispardhaa pesh nahin kar sakate
 More players are comfortable and are well aware that there is no competition for them at the top level
 prashn: team ko england main kahaan pareshaani hui
 Should he have played more matches before the Lord's Test? uttar: jab team asia se baahar ja rahi ho to yah kaaphi ahm he ki pehle test match se purv paristhitiyon se saamanjasy baitaane ke liye use paryaapt match abhyaas mili
 The situation is quite different from the West Indies to England
 shrinkhalaa kaa pehla test adhikansh samay haarane vaali team kaa shrinkhalaa main bhagya tay kar detaa he
 This degrades the morale of the team and cannot be overcome without an exceptional performance
 prashn: jab aap vahaan the to kya dhoni kii captaini se khush the
 Or did you think he could do better with the fielders
 uttar: captain kya kar saktaa he jab mukhya gendbaaj choton se jujh rahe hon or ahm kaich tapakaae ja rahe hon
 He made it clear by bowling, leaving his wicketkeeping gloves at Lord's
 prashn: rahul dravid ne pehle do test main behtareen ballebaaji kii or shuruuaat main vivies lakshmana ne bhi
 Sachin Tendulkar also showed his status
 kya aapako lagata he ki samay aa gaya he ki in diggajon ke jane ke baad team ke bhavishya ke bare main vichaar kiya jaye or rohit sharma tathaa viraat kohli jaise khilaadiyon ko taiyaar kiya jaye
 Answer: Of course
 chayankartaaon kaa kaam hi pratibha kii pahchaan karke use nikhaarana he
 They should show future plans
 antim ekadash koi bhi chun saktaa he lekin vikalpon kaa kya hoga
 The problem is right here
 rohit or viraat se aage bhi khilaadiyon ko dhundne kii jarurat he
 Everything is fine as long as you are winning but be prepared for any outcome
 7wein vetan ayog kii report ko lagu hue kai maheene biit gaye hai
 After several objections from the employees' unions, the government started discussing the formation of committees
 in samitiyon ko karmchaariyon kii samasya kaa samaadhaan chaar maheenon main karnaa tha lekin ab tak saat maheene biit chuke hai
 It is now reported that one of the three committees formed by the government, which also had the issue of allowance, has finalized its report and soon this committee will submit its report to the Ministry of Finance
 sutron kaa kahana he ki yah report 22 farvari ke baad sarkaar ko saunpi ja sakati he

 saath hi in karmchaaree netaaon kaa kahana he ki sarkaar karmchaariyon ke saath taalamatol kaa ravaiya apana rahi he
 The report which should have been given to the government in four months is not ready yet
 karmchaaree is baat se bhi naaraaz hai ki unhen lagata he ki sarkaar karmchaariyon ko bhatta dene main bhi jaanboojhkar deree kar rahi he
 Central employees believe that giving increased allowance will put some additional burden on the state exchequer, hence the government is delaying these matters

 in samitiyon ne vetan ayog kii report par charchaaen kii , lekin abhi tak kuch bhi sakaaratmak parinaam saamne nahin aayaa he

 pradhanmantri narendra modi do din ke gujarat daure par hai
 PM Modi, who visited Gujarat, got a different look on Tuesday
 gujarat ke adalaj main ek kaarykram ke dauraan ek hi manch par pradhanmantri narendra modi or gujarat ke purv mukhyamantri keshubhai patel maujuud the
 During this time Narendra Modi was guarding all the leaders
 jab piem modi keshubhai patel ke paas pahunche to unhone keshubhai patel ke pair chhukar aashirwad liya
 On the second day of his Gujarat visit, Prime Minister Narendra Modi reached the stage on Tuesday to lay the foundation stone of the Panchadhatu Temple and Teaching Bhawan and Vidyarthi Bhawan to be built in Annapurnadham Adalaj, the temple of Kuldevi Annapurna Maa of Leuva Patel
 isi dauraan manch par maujuud purv mukhyamantri keshubhai patel ko piem modi ne dekha or jhuk kar unke pair chhue
 Actually Prime Minister Narendra Modi considers Keshubhai Patel as his political guru
 pradhanmantri jahaan manch par sabhi se haath mila rahe the, vahiin keshubhai patel ke pair chune ke saath hi sabha main maujuud sabhi logon ne taaliyon ke saath unka abhivadan kiya
 Not only this, Prime Minister Narendra Modi stayed with Keshubhai and also talked for a while with him
 pradhanmantri ne keshubhai kii tabiyat ke bare main bhi jaankaree lee
 Keshubhai himself comes from the Leuva Patidar society
 aise main keshubhai ke pair choona pradhanmantri kaa ek sandesh dena bhi tha ki aaj bhi unke dil main leuva patel samaaj ke liye utana hi prem he jitna pehle tha
 This is not the first time the Prime Minister has touched Keshubhai's feet on stage
 isse pehle bhi narendra modi gujarat ke mukhyamantri ke taur par apana istipha dene ke baad pradhanmantri pad ke liye shapath grahan karne ja rahe the, tab bhi unhone keshubhai ke pair chhukar unka aashirwad liya tha
 Significantly, after the earthquake in 2001, Narendra Modi became Chief Minister of Gujarat after Keshubhai resigned as Chief Minister
 isse pehle keshubhai or narendra modi ke bich main matbhed kii kai khabaren bhi aa chuki hai
 Keshubhai formed his own Gujarat Parivartan Party in 2012 and also contested elections
 haalanki, keshubhai kii party kii taraf se chunaav ladane vaale sabhi log haar gaye the, sirf keshubhai ore nalin kotdia hi chunaav jeet paae the
 Within a period of time, Keshubhai merged his Gujarat Parivartan Party with the BJP
 haalanki 2012 ke baad keshubhai sakriy raajnneeti main bhi nahi rahe hai lekin bataur guru ke taur par pradhanmantri narendra modi aaj bhi unako apana guru maanate hai
 Perhaps this is the reason why the Prime Minister on the stage touched Keshubhai Patel's feet and took his blessings
 samachar agency eenai ne iskaa video jari kiya he
 It is seen in this video that during an event in the court of Gandhinagar district, PM Modi went to the stage in front of Keshubhai Patel in order to meet all the leaders and he took blessings by touching the feet of former Gujarat Chief Minister Keshubhai Patel
 is dauraan vah kuch baaten bhi karte najar aa rahe hai
 When PM Modi was touching the feet of Keshubhai Patel, Keshubhai Patel had a strange feeling on his face
 isse pehle pradhanmantri narendra modi ne ahmedabad main ek sabha ko sambodhit karne ke baad der shaam raisen gaanv pahunche jahaan unhone apni 90 varshiya maa se somvaar ko mulaakaat bhi kii
 Before meeting his mother, Modi went to the famous Dholeshwar Mahadev temple near Raisen and offered prayers there on the occasion of Mahashivaratri

 Here farmers are using liquor richly in potato fields
 aalu kisaanon kaa kahana he ki sharaab ke chhidkaav se aalu kaa growth bahut teji se badhata he
 Farmers in the district are spraying liquor in the fields for higher potato production

 Also, the potato size is also thicker, which leads to higher profits

 Farmers also say that the potato crop gets ready quickly with alcohol spray

 Due to excess frost in the cold, potatoes are sprayed with alcohol
 is bare main baharich ke udyaan nireekshak aarake verma ne enditivi ko bataaya ki iskaa koi vaigyanik aadhaar nahin he
